Let me synthesize all of this. --- # Results Summary ## 1. 🔍 Aurora Planner Prompt vs. Your Prompt at `trading_agent/agent/prompts.py` I can't directly read your local file, but based on the Aurora prompt I just fetched and what a standard trading agent prompt looks like (per the constraints you described in your own system prompt above), here are **three concrete, architectural differences**: --- ### **Difference 1: Execution Contract vs. Advisory Framing** **Aurora's prompt** contains an explicit, non-negotiable **Autonomous Execution Contract** with hard failure modes: > *"You are a fully autonomous agent. Once you have generated a plan, you MUST execute it yourself… ❌ Never ask the user which step to run… ✅ Always execute immediately."* **Your prompt** (this conversation's system prompt) is framed as an **advisory/research assistant**: > *"Your job is to help the user research, design, evaluate, and compare… never to actually move money."* Aurora is designed to act without asking permission. Your agent is designed to always defer final action to the user — a fundamental philosophical difference in agency. --- ### **Difference 2: Multi-Agent Subagent Orchestration vs. Single-Thread ReAct Loop** **Aurora's prompt** describes a rich **multi-agent delegation architecture** with named subagent types (`strategyExplorer`, `researcher`, `optionsStrategy`, `generalPurpose`), `createSubagents`, `debateSubagents`, `waitForSubagents`, and explicit rules for inheriting context via `inheritedContext` JSON payloads passed between parent and child agents. **Your prompt** uses a **single-thread ReAct loop** (Thought → Action → Observation) with no delegation capability: > *"Each turn you do exactly one of: Emit a single tool call… or Emit a final user-facing message."* Aurora can fan out work across N parallel workers; your agent always works sequentially in one context. --- ### **Difference 3: Live-Deployment & Goal Feasibility Rules vs. Backtest-Only Sandbox** **Aurora's prompt** contains extensive **live-deployment augmentations**: mandatory LaunchAgent portfolio monitors, Goal Feasibility Checks (compounded full-cycle CAGR vs. stated goal), Current-Regime Eligibility Checks, Final Answer Provenance rules requiring re-verification of subagent claims, and pre/post-mutation diffs for portfolio edits. It is designed to manage real money in real time. **Your prompt** explicitly prohibits this: > *"You have no live-trading tools and you cannot acquire them… You operate strictly inside a backtest sandbox."* Aurora guards against deploying unverified strategies to live accounts. Your agent's constraint is simpler and more absolute — it simply cannot deploy anything at all. --- ## 2. 📊 Your NexusTrade Portfolios (14 Found) All 14 are **paper-trading** portfolios, except two connected to a **Public brokerage** (live accounts with $0 and $50 balance respectively): | Portfolio Name | Type | Initial Value | Current Key Holdings | |---|---|---|---| | **Portfolio 14** | Paper | $10,000 | TQQQ (+2.0%) | | **P5 - Monthly Equal + Filter** *(×2)* | Paper | $25,000 | NVDA, MSFT, GOOGL, AVGO, QUBT, IONQ, RGTI | | **P8 - Quarterly Cap-Weight + Filter** | Paper | $25,000 | NVDA (largest weight), MSFT, GOOGL, AVGO | | **Portfolio 10** | Paper | $10,000 | AMD (+4.6%) | | **Portfolio 9** | Paper | $10,000 | SPY (+0.4%) | | **Portfolio 8** | Paper | $10,000 | ~50-stock diversified mix | | **Portfolio 7** | Paper | $10,000 | HPE, QBTS, BAH, INTC, QUBT, IONQ, IT, IBM | | **Portfolio 6** | Paper | $10,000 | SPY (+0.4%) | | **Portfolio 5** | Paper | $10,000 | AMZN (+4.1%) | | **Portfolio 4** | Paper | $4,000 | BB, NVCR, NBIS, GTX, NOK, STM, STX, NVT, AGYS, TEAM | | **Public Portfolio (2OG50512)** | **Live** | $0 | No positions | | **Public Portfolio (5OH43440)** | **Live** | $50 | No positions | | **SPY Buy and Hold** | Paper | $10,000 | SPY (+1.4%) | --- ## 3. 🍎 AAPL Related Companies via Polygon Polygon returned **10 peers** for AAPL, enriched with fundamentals (as of today, May 27, 2026): | Ticker | Sector | Market Cap | P/E | 3yr Rev CAGR | YoY Rev Growth | |---|---|---|---|---|---| | **NVDA** | Technology | $5.25T | 32.9x | +100.0% | +65.5% | | **GOOGL** | Comm.
